|2.0|http://wordpress.org/export/1.2/excerpt/|http://purl.org/rss/1.0/modules/content/|http://wellformedweb.org/CommentAPI/|http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/|http://wordpress.org/export/1.2/|medagg|https://medagghealthcare.com|United towards a healthy tomorrow|Mon, 17 Nov 2025 17:31:01 +0000|en-US|1.2|https://medagghealthcare.com|https://medagghealthcare.com|2|Medagg|info@medagghealthcare.com|Medagg Health Care|Medagg|Health Care|https://wordpress.org/?v=6.8.3|https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/cropped-android-chrome-192x192-1-32x32.png|medagg|https://medagghealthcare.com|32|32|Goal to become the Airbnb in healthcare is what made Medagg possible says Ramesh Krishnan.......| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<h3>Goal to become the Airbnb in healthcare is what made Medagg possible says Ramesh Krishnan, Board Member, Sahyadri Hospitals and Dr. Rela Institute and Medical centre and Managing Partner at MEDAGG VENTURES LLP</h3> &nbsp;  <img class="alignleft wp-image-16633" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/rendezvous-with-ramesh-krishnan-300x169.jpg" alt="" width="414" height="233" />  &nbsp;  <em class="h5 text-dark"><img src="https://medicircle.in/images/quote.png" />“The buying behaviour in which people are buying healthcare services is constantly changing. This is one of the reasons I say that the industry is nowhere near steady state,” says Ramesh Krishnan, Board Member, Sahyadri Hospitals and Dr. Rela Institute and Medical centre and Managing Partner at MEDAGG VENTURES LLP.<img src="https://medicircle.in/images/quoterev.png" /></em>  &nbsp;  &nbsp;  &nbsp;  Data aggregation is the process of combining information from multiple databases to produce cohesive, shareable information. When it comes to healthcare data, the benefits of sharing are plentiful as from pharmaceutical and biotech companies to care providers, the healthcare sector demands evidence-based decision-making now more than ever.  <strong>Ramesh Krishnan, Board Member, Sahyadri Hospitals,</strong> which is a large West India chain of Hospitals. He is also a board member of Dr. Rela Institute and Medical centre, Managing Partner at MEDAGG VENTURES LLP, and the Operating Partner at Ever stone Capital.  <b>Medaag Ventures LLP </b>is a team of experts who specialize in operations and management, strategic consulting, and transaction advisory services in the healthcare industry.  <b>Medagg Venture’s goal to become the Airbnb in healthcare</b><b> </b>Ramesh throws light on the subject, “<b><i>Medical Aggregation was the theme that Medagg as a firm was founded on. We work on aggregation at various levels. The eventual goal would be to become Airbnb in healthcare by aggregating secondary neighborhood hospitals. To this end, we have already put together a pipeline of hospitals and are in the process of raising funds.</i></b><i> In the meantime, we also apply the principles of medical aggregations in a few more areas as well. For example, we run channel partnerships for a few innovative startups in the healthcare space which help aggregate specific healthcare services across multiple hospitals from a central command centre. ER, ICU, e-pharmacy, central procurement, etc are a few to name. </i><b><i>We also partner with a few innovative service providers in commoditizing some common but underprovided treatments like varicose veins by bringing about scale. This we believe could become a huge game-changer in the daycare space</i></b>,” he says.  &nbsp;  <b>Bringing value addition to hospital operations</b>  Ramesh explains<b>, “Medagg also runs strategic advisory services and Transaction advisory services which again focus on bringing value addition to hospital operations through aggregation concepts</b>. I feel that the secondary hospital market is so fragmented that consolidation is inevitable for that segment of the market even to survive. This is the reason we focus so heavily on the aggregation as a theme. It is ironic that at a time when the country needs more treatment beds, one segment of the already installed beds (secondary hospitals) are struggling for survival since they are sub-scale and are not able to handle costs. This actually makes it an ideal case for consolidation,” he says  <b>A journey of more than 25 years in the Pharmaceutical and Healthcare industry</b> <blockquote>Ramesh talks about his journey, “<b><i>Healthcare has always been a very fulfilling profession for me. In fact, moving from Pharma to Healthcare delivery has been even more gratifying because you are directly connected to patients. There is so much more that could and must be done in this industry which is still not near equilibrium when it behaves like a steady-state. After 25 years in large corporate, I felt that I could contribute more in the affordable healthcare segment by aggregating services if I go out on my own and that is how Medagg was born</i></b>,” he says.</blockquote> <b>Healthcare nowhere near steady-state</b><b> </b>Ramesh shares his thoughts on the future outcomes we should watch out for in terms of Healthcare, “<b><i>The buying behavior in which people are buying healthcare services is constantly changing. This is one of the reasons I say that the industry is nowhere near steady-state</i></b>. <i>The penetration of insurance is still below 50% in the country. Insurance still does not cover daycare and outpatient treatments. This is primarily because of the fact that primary and secondary healthcare segments are still very fragmented and run like mom-and-pop stores with no large corporate chains having established presence as yet. These are inevitable changes that are bound to come about in the coming few years. These will help consolidate and organize the primary and secondary healthcare segments. A number of startups with interesting products and services are springing up of late, which will all aid to bring about this consolidation. T</i><b><i>he number of people buying healthcare online is also constantly on the increase. An OYO or Airbnb kind of consolidation in the healthcare space is bound to happen as this would become a basic line of survival for many struggling secondary hospitals. The hospital wards are continuing to be extended out to peoples’ homes with homecare constantly on the increase. This is not only increasing the availability of beds in hospitals in a country that is below global averages in bed provision but also reducing the level of hospital-acquired infections. The government has made its intentions clear that it wants to provide healthcare to its entire population of 1.3 billion people. But it has also made it clear that it will remain as a payor and will not get into provision. The provision is left to the private sector to fulfill. In a social industry like healthcare where the government takes the role of a payor and leaves the provision to the private players, price regulations become a norm. We have started seeing this already and this will only increase. This will call for more innovation to be rolled out in this space. So with this entire churn happening in the industry, we can expect a very exciting, challenging, and innovative decade ahead for Indian healthcare</i></b><i>,</i>” he says.  &nbsp;  <b>The medical fraternity more confident in handling the sick due to COVID</b>  Ramesh presents his views, “<b><i>It is true that COVID is not going away in any hurry. But it is also true that our medical fraternity has become a lot more confident in handling the sick. To be honest, I am keener to see an established line of treatment for the disease than even the vaccine. So the fact that our doctors are a lot more confident in treating patients is actually good news. While COVID has indeed established a new normal in the way we go about doing our day-to-day activities, I also see a huge opportunity for innovation, especially within the healthcare space. We will of course have to take the obvious precautions before we get out of this pandemic fully. We cannot drop our guard as yet. However, I do see things coming back quite quickly albeit with caution,</i></b>” he says.|5761|2022-03-17 19:40:37|2022-03-17 19:40:37|closed|closed|voice-of-healthcare|publish|0|0|blog_post||0|post_tag|medagg|Medagg|_edit_lock|1715324106:2| |

| | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |STARTUP JOURNEY OF MEDAGG!| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="wp-image-16631 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/1647365708371-300x197.jpeg" alt="" width="495" height="325" />  We started off 3 years ago with “Medical Aggregation" in mind.All we knew was that this theme made sense given how fragmented the medical services industry was and still is.  The Consulting vertical proved to be the best conduit to bring potential aggregation ideas to fruition.  We branched off into Transaction Advisory seeing the need for fund raising amongst businesses who wish to consolidate / aggregate.  In the process we stumbled upon business in which we got so engrossed and involved that we made Strategic Investments ourselves! We are now proud to be part of the below portfolio.  But we have stayed our course in developing our own aggregation platform as well. <strong>Medagg Healthcare</strong> is emerging as the largest search engine platform for secondary hospitals in Tamil Nadu.|16015|2022-04-08 17:57:39|2022-04-08 17:57:39|closed|closed|startup-journey-of-medagg|publish|0|0|blog_post||0|post_tag|medagg|Medagg|_edit_lock|1688100497:2| |

| | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |Pain Doesn't Have to be a Part of Your Life!| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |&nbsp;  <img class="size-full wp-image-21211 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Piles-2.png" alt="" width="800" height="450" />  Piles, are also called Haemorrhoids, are enlarged blood vessels that you can get inside or around your anus, which is the opening of the bottom.  It’s normal to have blood vessels in the anus, as they play an essential role in incontinence. But piles can develop if these blood vessels become enlarged. It is a lump that is found in that particular area. The size of the piles might vary from person to person. Piles can be internal or external too.  Internal piles are customarily located above the opening of the anus, and they are the more common type. External piles occur on the outside edge of the anus. <h5><strong>Table of Contents:</strong></h5><p id="A"></p> <ul>  	<li><a href="#A"><b>Types of Piles</b></a></li>  	<li><a href="#B"><b>Symptoms of Piles</b></a></li> <li><a href="#C"><b>Causes of Piles</b></a></li> <li><a href="#D"><b>Treatment for Piles</b></a></li> <li><a href="#E"><b>Minimally Invasive Procedures</b></a></li> <li><a href="#F"><b>What is the leading cause of piles</b></a></li> <li><a href="#G"><b>How do I know if I have piles?</b></a></li> <li><a href="#H"><b>How do piles go away?</b></a></li> <li><a href="#I"><b>What foods cause piles?</b></a></li> </ul> <p id="B"></p> <h6><strong>Types Of Piles</strong></h6> There are by far two types of hemorrhoids which are Internal and External.  <strong>Internal Piles</strong>  Internal piles are so far inside the rectum that you can’t usually see or feel them. However, they don’t generally hurt because of a few pain-sensing nerves there. They are not visible to the naked eyes. <p id="C"></p> <strong>External Piles</strong> External piles get formed in the anal region and create discomfort. When an external haemorrhoid protrudes through the anus, it can be seen and felt. Sometimes blood clots can form within the mass that slips down; it can be harrowing. <h6><strong>Symptoms Of Piles</strong></h6> Internal piles rarely cause pain, and they typically can’t be felt unless they collapse. Many people with internal haemorrhoids don’t know they have them because they don’t have symptoms.  If a person has internal piles symptoms, they might see blood on toilet paper, stool, or toilet bowl. These are signs of rectal bleeding. <h6><strong>Signs Of External Piles Include:</strong></h6> <ul>  	<li>Itchy anus</li>  	<li>Hard lumps near the anus that feel sore</li>  	<li>Pain or ache in the anus, especially while sitting</li>  	<li>Rectal bleeding</li> </ul> <p id="D"></p> <h6><strong>Causes Of Piles</strong></h6> Straining puts pressure on veins in the anus or rectum, causing haemorrhoids. Any straining that increases pressure on the belly or lower extremities can cause anal and rectal veins to become swollen and inflamed. Haemorrhoids may develop due to: <ul>  	<li>Pelvic pressure from weight gain, especially during pregnancy.</li>  	<li>Pushing hard to have a bowel movement due to constipation.</li>  	<li>Straining to lift heavy objects or weightlifting.</li> </ul> <p id="E"></p> <h6><strong>Treatment For Piles</strong></h6> <strong>Non-Surgical Medication</strong>  Several therapeutic options are available to make symptoms more manageable for an individual with piles.  <strong>Over-The-Counter (OTC)</strong>  These are available over-the-counter or online. Medications include painkillers, ointments, creams, and pads to help soothe redness and swelling around the anus. OTC remedies do not cure piles but can relieve the symptoms. Please do not use them for more than seven days in a row, as they can cause further irritation of the area and thinness of the skin. Also, do not use two or more medications simultaneously unless advised by a medical professional.  <strong>Corticosteroids</strong>  These can reduce inflammation and pain.  <strong>Laxatives</strong>  The doctor may prescribe laxatives if a person with piles suffers from constipation. These can help the person pass stools more efficiently and reduce pressure on the lower colon. <h6><strong>Minimally Invasive Procedures</strong></h6> For continuous bleeding or painful haemorrhoids, the doctor might recommend one of the minimally invasive procedures available. These treatments can be done in your doctor’s office or different outpatient settings and don’t usually require anaesthesia.  <strong>Rubber Band Ligation</strong>  The doctor places one or two tiny rubber bands around the internal haemorrhoid to cut off its circulation. The haemorrhoid shrinks and falls off within a week. Haemorrhoid banding can be uncomfortable and cause bleeding, which is rarely severe.  <strong>Injection (Sclerotherapy)</strong>  The specialist injects a chemical solution into the haemorrhoid tissue to shrink it. While the injection causes little or no pain, it might be less effective than rubber band ligation.  <strong>Coagulation (Infrared, Laser Or Bipolar)</strong> Coagulation techniques use laser or infrared light or heat. They cause slight, bleeding internal haemorrhoids to harden and wither.  <strong>Warm Bath</strong>  Warm baths can help soothe irritation from haemorrhoids. Using a sitz bath, a small plastic tub that fits over a toilet seat can immerse the affected area. Trying a warm or sitz bath for 20 minutes after each bowel movement and Adding Epsom salt to the tub can provide further relief.  <strong>Cold Compress</strong>  Applying ice packs or cold compresses to the anus can relieve swelling for 15 minutes at a time. For large, painful haemorrhoids, cold compresses can be highly effective. Make sure to wrap ice inside a cloth or paper towel. Never apply something frozen directly to your skin since this can harm or damage the skin.  <strong>Do Not Scratch</strong>  Scratching damages the skin and worsens the irritation and itching.  <strong>Apply Coconut Oil</strong>  Coconut oil is a natural moisturiser that may also help with haemorrhoid symptoms. In addition, applying coconut oil may reduce the irritation and swelling, and it may also help reduce the urge to scratch.  <strong>Try Squat</strong><p id="F"></p>  Try a squat position. For example, put a short bench under your feet when you go to the bathroom. Raising your knees as you sit on the toilet changes the position of your inner workings and could make bowel movements easier. <h6><b>Conclusion</b></h6><p id="G"></p> Understanding the common anal and rectal conditions of piles is essential for effective management, including piles treatment and haemorrhoids prevention. By being aware of the causes, symptoms, treatment options, and prevention tips, individuals can take proactive steps towards maintaining anal and rectal health. Remember, if you have any concerns or questions, it is always advisable to consult a healthcare professional for further guidance and support. Take control of your well-being and prioritise your digestive health. <h6><b>People Also Ask</b></h6><p id="H"></p> <b>1. What Is The Leading Cause Of Piles?</b> Piles occur due to chronic constipation, chronic diarrhoea, lifting heavy weights, pregnancy, or straining when passing a stool.  <b>2. How Do I Know If I Have Piles?</b><p id="I"></p> A person with piles may experience the feeling that the bowels are still full after passing a stool. Bright red blood is visible after a bowel movement. The area around the anus is itchy, red, and sore. Pain occurs during the passing of a stool.  <b>3. How Do Piles Go Away?</b> There is no set duration for haemorrhoids. Small haemorrhoids may clear up without any treatment within a few days. Large, external haemorrhoids may take longer to heal and cause significant pain and discomfort. If haemorrhoids have not resolved within a few days, it is best to see a doctor for treatment.  <b>4. What Foods Cause Piles?</b> Foods with little fibre can cause constipation (and therefore haemorrhoids) worse, so it’s best to limit how much you eat of them. <ul>  	<li>White bread</li>  	<li>Milk, cheese, and other dairies</li>  	<li>Meat</li>  	<li>Processed foods such as frozen meals and fast food</li> </ul> Watch the amount of salt you consume because It can lead to your body hanging on to water, putting more pressure on your blood vessels. That includes the veins in your bottom that cause haemorrhoids.  &nbsp; <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="#book-appointment"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-21216 size-large" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/VOXAGE-Consultancy-2-1024x256.png" alt="" width="800" height="200" /></a></p> &nbsp;  &nbsp;  <script type="application/ld+json">{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"FAQPage","mainEntity":[{"@type":"Question","name":"1.) | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |Understanding Anal Fissures: Causes, Symptoms, and Treatment Options| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="size-full wp-image-21211 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/website-backdrop.png" alt="" width="800" height="450" />  Anal fissures are the ruptures or tears of the conjunction of the anal channels through the last part of your colon and the stools from the body. A few symptoms are commonly associated with bowel movements, such as itching, bleeding, and pain. In some cases, small fissures that cause pain can heal on their own, however, if there are deeper fissures that are chronic, a physician may need to treat them. &amp;nsb,  An anal fissure is very common among infants and children but can affect people of any age. In general, anal fission heals within four to six weeks. However, if the rift fails to heal during this period, it may become chronic and medical or surgical treatment will be necessary to cure the anal rift. <h6><b>Table of Content:</b></h6> <ul>  	<li><b>Symptoms of Anal Fissure</b></li> </ul> &nbsp; <ul>  	<li><b>Causes of Anal Fissure</b></li> </ul> &nbsp; <ul>  	<li><b>Home Remedies for Anal Fissure</b></li> </ul> &nbsp; <ul>  	<li><b>Is Fissure Curable Without Surgery?</b></li> </ul> &nbsp; <ul>  	<li><b>Which is the best treatment for fissures?</b></li> </ul> <h6><b>Symptoms of Anal Fissure</b></h6> Anal Fissure occurs when the anal canal is damaged in some way. The trauma to the anal lining can lead to symptoms such as <ul>  	<li>Discomfort</li>  	<li>Itching</li>  	<li>Pain with bowel movements</li>  	<li>Bleeding</li> </ul> <h6><b>Causes Of Anal Fissure</b></h6> Some trauma in the anal channel causes it. These tears or rupturing of the rectum can happen to anyone, but it is usually seen in the younger and healthier. Anal stenosis is generally caused by pressure on the anal cavity; the reasons could be sitting for a long time, being stressed, or having a high-pressure job. Primary fissures are simple fractures.  A fissure may be caused by severe constipation, high pressure on the anal cavity muscles such as long driving in everyday life, etc. They may occur during childbirth or after a difficult childbirth. Earlier, it was thought that most fissures were caused by straining to pass the stools and uncomfortable bowel movements. However, now it is known that the tone of the sphincter muscle can cause chronic fissures. Excessive pressure on the anal hole may cause these, and it may become a more painful and stressful life, and spasms and breakdowns may become chronic.  Some conditions that are commonly associated with primary anal fissures include <ul>  	<li>Chronic Constipation</li>  	<li>Hypothyroidism</li>  	<li>Obesity</li>  	<li>Tumours</li> </ul> Additionally, some of the minor common causes of the same phenomenon are as follows: <ul>  	<li>Anal cancer</li>  	<li>Crohn’s disease and inflammatory bowel disease such as Ulcerative Colitis</li>  	<li>HIV/AIDS</li>  	<li>Tuberculosis</li> </ul> <h6><b>Home Remedies For Anal Fissure</b></h6> Natural Remedies  <b>1. Sitz bath</b> It means sitting in a bathtub with lukewarm water to reduce the pain and get relief, but it may not accelerate the healing of the anal fissure. These plastic baths can be purchased from local drug stores on any available online platforms, are filled with water and are usually recommended for using a tub for approximately 10 to 15 minutes, preferably 2-3 times a day. Doctors prescribe some medications or Epsom salt as an addition to water. These additives help reduce pain, itch, remove discomfort, and clear the infection. You can use your bathtub if you don’t have access to a plastic sitz bath. If you soak in a bathtub, be sure to clean it well before sitting in it, and keep to the recommended soaking time.  <b>2. Include Fibre Rich Food</b> Include plenty of high-fibre foods such as beans, split peas, lentils, chickpeas, bran cereal, pumpkin seeds, soya beans, and whole grains. Also, eat prunes and raisins that help soften stools. A soft, easily passed stool will be less painful on the fissure and stop it from becoming grave and irritated. Some Examples of High Fiber Foods Include <ul>  	<li>High fibre bran cereal</li>  	<li>Beans (kidney, yellow, white)</li>  	<li>Split peas</li>  	<li>Chickpeas</li>  	<li>Lentils</li>  	<li>Pumpkin seeds</li>  	<li>Soybeans</li>  	<li>Avocado</li> </ul> <b>3. Fibre Supplement</b> If you don’t get enough fibre from food, a fibre supplement may help. There are many different types of fibre supplements, with some of the most common ingredients being psyllium husk, methylcellulose, and polycarbophil. Consult a nutritionist and take a balanced diet with a fibre supplement to benefit from the supplement. It is suggested to start fibre supplements slowly and gradually increase the amount daily to avoid side effects such as coating and gas. In addition, fibre supplements can help with other health complications, such as constipation and diarrhoea.  <b>4. Stool Softener</b> A stool softener may help to relieve constipation. Stool softeners are not laxatives, and they are usually considered safe. Though they may have negligible side effects, it is still important to speak with a doctor before using one. These agents help increase the amount of water drawn into the digestive tract or intestines, making the stool softer. There are many types of stool softeners available as tablets and liquids. Stool softeners are typically used for seven days. Other methods that can be followed to help with constipation to help discontinue the stool softeners include changing your lifestyle habits. Also, talk to your doctor or healthcare provider about the over-the-counter stool softener that you can use.  <b>5. Stay Hydrated</b> Staying hydrated will help overcome the problem of constipation. Drinking sufficient water can help keep the stools soft and easier to pass. Foods rich in water content can also contribute to your water intake goal. Foods rich in water also contribute to water intake goals. The amount of water you need each day depends on your weight and gender and varies from person to person, but on average, men should drink about 13 cups and women about 9 cups. More water is needed after physical activity, especially after exercise or when pregnant or breastfeeding. Your body is the only one that can tell you how much water you need. When the stool is soft and easy to pass, you’ve had enough water in a day.  <b>6. Follow the bathroom hygiene.</b> After each bowel movement, clean the area around the anus gently and dry it thoroughly. If you have the urge to pass stools, don’t ignore it. If you try to control your urge to defecate, it will worsen the fissure. Do not use soap or take bubble baths as they can irritate the skin in the anal canal. Avoid excessive pressure or sitting on the toilet for a long time if it puts extra pressure on the anal area. <h6><b>Laser treatment for Fissure</b></h6> If none of the remedies worked, it is ideal for getting the laser done. Consult your healthcare provider and seek their help for laser treatment to get rid of the fissure. <h6><b>Conclusion</b></h6> Understanding the common anal and rectal conditions of Fissure is essential for effective management, including fissure treatment. By being aware of the causes, symptoms, treatment options, and prevention tips, individuals can take proactive steps towards maintaining anal and rectal health. Remember, if you have any concerns or questions, it is always advisable to consult a healthcare professional for further guidance and support. Take control of your well-being and prioritise your digestive health <h6><b>People Also Ask:</b></h6> <b>1. | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |FISTULA| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="size-full wp-image-21211 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/website-backdrop-1.png" alt="" width="800" height="450" /> <h6>Overview</h6> An abnormal connection, such as one between a blood vessel and another structure or an organ and another body area, is called a fistula. Injury or surgery are the usual causes of fistulas. However, a fistula can also develop due to an infection or inflammation.  Different areas or portions of the human body might develop fistulae. Fistulas can also form in other areas of the body, such as between the throat and neck, the colon and the skin nearby, an artery and vein, etc. An infected tunnel between the anus and the perianal skin is an anal fistula. The anal opening is where this canal’s exterior entrance is located.  The individual is encouraged to drink plenty of liquids, especially water, and to eat a balanced, high-fibre diet in cases of anal fistula. This results in developing a soft stool and lessening the pressure needed to pass stools. Passing a firm stool can be highly unpleasant and challenging for people with such illnesses. When using the restroom, the patient should maintain their hygiene. Infections with the disease already present and other problems can result from unhygienic conditions.  <b>Anal Fistula:</b> An anal fistula is used to describe the infected tube that forms between the anus and the perianal skin. The anal opening is where the fistula’s one end is located. A fistula is typically discovered in a person who had an anal abscess earlier. A fistula can also be brought on by other severe conditions like Crohn’s disease, cancer, warts, radiation, trauma, etc. Fistula is typically a complaint of an obese person who spends a lot of time sitting and doesn’t engage in regular physical activity. Adults are more likely than children to get a fistula. A substantial risk of anal fistula exists in people who have perianal abscesses. <h6>Symptoms</h6> <ul>  	<li>Anal opening, in particular, is surrounded by pain, swelling, itching, irritation, or sore skin.</li>  	<li>Discharge of blood</li>  	<li>Bowel movements that hurt. In the later stages of the illness, the patient may also express pain while urinating.</li>  	<li>Fever and exhaustion</li>  	<li>discharge with a foul odour coming from the anal aperture</li> </ul> <h6>Home Remedies For Anal Fistula</h6> <b>The Top 7 Home Treatments for Anal Fistula Include: Sitz Bath</b>  One of the greatest ways to treat anal fistula symptoms, which include irritation, swelling, pain, and inflammation, is to take a sitz bath. Anal area bathing in simple, warm water is known as a sitz bath. The water shouldn’t be too hot. A fistula patient should sitz bathe at least three to four times daily. (Read about the advantages of sitz baths and how to take one here)  <b>Healthy food</b>  Keep your stomach and digestive system healthy by watching what you eat. Improve digestive conditions that are less susceptible to issues by avoiding hot, junk, and fatty foods. Increase your intake of whole grains, leafy greens, fruits, and lean meats. Constipation can irritate a fistula, so eating more fibre-rich foods like cereal will help you prevent it. You can employ a few kitchen tricks to relieve fistula symptoms, including: <ul>  	<li>Honey: Honey has antibacterial properties, and regular ingestion benefits overall health. One tablespoon of honey should be combined with a glass of warm water.</li>  	<li>Oregano Oil: You can cure fistulas using oregano oil. Antibacterial, antiviral, antibiotic, and anti-inflammatory activities are present in the oil.</li>  	<li>One spoonful of ground flaxseed powder should be added to a glass of water. Then, before going to bed, give it a good stir. It aids in controlling bowel movements.</li> </ul> <b>Drink water</b>  One of the finest home remedies for fistula is to drink lots of water. Avoid soda and alcohol; drink a ton of water and fruit juices. Ginger tea, turmeric milk, etc., are options. Constipation strains your fistula; therefore, doing this will prevent it. In addition, a surplus of water will soften waste and assist in intestinal cleaning.  <b>Use donut pillows</b>  Avoid the added pressure on your back, buttocks, and legs if your toilet job requires you to sit down for extended periods, especially if you have an anal fistula. This might be achieved by using a “donut pillow” instead of a standard chair or simply sitting on the toilet seat.  <b>Maintain proper bathroom hygiene</b>  After using the bathroom or having a bowel movement, always wash your anal area. The first step in preventing an illness is to avoid any bacteria that may still be present on your skin. Always carry wipes while outside in the open and if you can’t wash them. Because they come into contact with germs the most, your hands need to be cleaned frequently. If the fistula leaks throughout the day, change your underwear as needed. This will stop the growth of bacteria and the spread of germs, which can lessen perianal irritation and assist in eliminating the bothersome symptoms related to fistulas.  <b>Strengthen your immunity</b> A nutritious diet that includes foods high in omega-3s, omega-6s, and vitamin C, such as fish, olive oil, and citrus fruits, will help you build a stronger immune system and reduce any inflammation fistula could bring on. <h6>When To See A Doctor</h6> <h6>People Also Ask</h6> <b>1. Can a fistula repair itself?</b> Anal fistulas typically do not heal on their own, necessitating surgery to treat them.  <b>2. What food cures fistula?</b> People with fistulas should consume lots of water and include fibre-rich foods in their daily diet. In addition, green leafy vegetables, fresh fruits, brown rice, and fish can be incorporated into their diet.  <b>3. What is the main cause of fistula?</b> Fistulas can develop as a result of inflammation or infection in addition to trauma or surgery. Fistulas are channels of infection that can occur when the lining of the intestine becomes ulcerated.  <b>Disclaimer:</b> We recommend consulting a Doctor before taking any action based on the above shared information.|21924|2023-07-20 10:20:21|2023-07-20 04:50:21|closed|closed|fistula|publish|0|0|blog_post||0| | | |_wds_readability|a:4:{s:5:"score";i:61;s:9:"raw_score";i:61;s:11:"is_readable";b:1;s:5:"error";b:0;}| |

| | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |TRANSFORMING MEDICAL AGGREGATION| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="size-full wp-image-21211 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/IMG_0971.jpg" alt="" width="800" height="450" /> Hospital discovery platform MEDAGG’s co-Founders Ramesh and Sumitha are adding clarity and sanity to the care experience for patients and end-users through the power of aggregating data, counselling and choice. <h3>BACKSTORY</h3> <a href="https://in.linkedin.com/in/ramesh-krishnan-522b477" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ramesh Krishnan</a> and <a href="https://in.linkedin.com/in/sumitha-karthik-b5a4344b" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Sumitha Karthik</a> are the Co-Founders of <a href="https://medagghealthcare.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Medagg Healthcare</a>, Tamil Nadu’s largest hospital discovery platform are on their way to transform patient experience in hospitals. Their platform makes the process of discovering healthcare options for elective procedures a whole new experience empowering patients with comprehensive information before making their choice. <h3>MEET THE CO-FOUNDERS</h3> Ramesh Krishnan is a seasoned healthcare management professional, who prior to founding Medagg, held key positions in the industry including that of South Asia CEO for IHH (Parkway Pantai). He was also the operating partner for the healthcare platform of Everstone capital and is an experienced M&amp;A professional. A HBS and IIFT Alumni, Ramesh has also spent close to 10 years of his professional life in key positions in the Pharma industry as well.  Sumitha Karthik is an Alumus of the Indian School of Business (ISB) and brings with her more than 20 years of experience in operations across the healthcare and aviation industries. She has run operations of Gleneagles global hospitals and Fortis hospitals apart from having been the head of crew operations across South India for Jet Airways.  We are honoured to have two stalwarts from the industry in our midst, and begin by probing into the core idea driving the journey. Below are excerpts from the exchange. <h3>THE BIG IDEA</h3> What is the one big concept or philosophy that defines you and your success mantra?  “<strong>Enabling everyone’s right to the right healthcare at the right cost is something that has been the passion of both of us and that is the sole reason for us to have enjoyed our journey in the healthcare industry. Playing a role in helping patients and patient families in finding this right healthcare option that suits their budget, their need and convenience, has been the guiding factor for founding Medagg which is short for Medical Aggregation.</strong>” <h3>EVOLUTION CURVE</h3> How did the concept snowball into the grand journey it is today? Any significant triggers or experiences catalysing it forward?  “We have as healthcare operators, had numerous people within friends and family, reaching out to us seeking guidance on how to locate the ideal hospital/healthcare provider. This gave us a realization that there are probably millions of people out there who do not have healthcare operators within their circles to reach out to for such informal advise. This is what led us to the idea of formalizing this advisory in the form of Medagg.” <h3>SOLVING FOR X</h3> All driven leaders have a burning target they want to crack. The x in the proverbial equation. What is your X?  “Medagg hopes to become the largest hospital discovery platform. We have started off with Tamil Nadu and have already aggregated more than 1000 hospitals in the state. We empower patients and patient families with the ease of searching alternate hospital options without the hassle of having to make personal visits to multiple hospitals or visit multiple websites. After all, in a world when Amazon and Swiggy have made “options” a part of everyone’s life and run successful businesses out of it, why would choice of hospitals not come into the hands of people?” <h3>THE DIFFERENTIATOR</h3> What’s unique about Medagg? What sets them apart from others in the market?  “As opposed to some of the recent surgery consolidation platforms which limit the number of affiliated hospitals per city,, Medagg works out of a much larger affiliation base of hospitals. We are across 9 cities and towns across the state of TN with more than 1000 affiliated hospital already. We host these options on a bilingual website / App. With its wide affiliation base of hospitals, Medagg is able to offer the patient a min of 3 options across any of the treatments, big and small. In the process, Medagg is also able to bring to the knowledge of the patient certain unique procedures and treatment modalities which otherwise may not be widely known <h3>USP’S OF MEDAGG</h3> Two unique characters have been incorporated in this process of helping the patient/family:  A -<strong>“Care Custodian”</strong> is a personal healthcare counsellor who helps the patient/family navigate and analyse the various options and eventually choose the right one.  B -<strong>“Care companion”</strong> is a personal assistant who will accompany the patient throughout the treatment journey.  Both the Custodians as well as the Companions are experienced hospital operators / healthcare workers who know the nuances of hospital operations and will hence be in a position to help the patient / family to navigate the various administrative steps during hospitalization. This helps the patient avoid common challenges like:  a.    Unexpected wait times for consultation.  b.    Unclear and vague treatment cost estimates from hospitals.  c.    Lack of clarity on insurance coverage.  d.    Frustrating admission and discharge processes.  e.    Lack of proper feedback from the hospital staff / doctors on the admitted patient’s progress. <h3>THE BROAD PICTURE</h3> We are curious about how MEDAGG fits in the context of the larger ecosystem scenario, and the leaders generously share their proprietary insights…  “In the larger context, even as India is still ramping up its available beds per capita,  the available beds as of today are mostly available in the small hospital (50 to 70 beds) segment. With the change in cost and price structures in the industry over the past several years, these small hospitals have been rendered unviable due to unit economics, unless they are single specialty units. Typically, the unit economics of multispecialty hospitals becomes viable for a capacity above 120 beds. In this scenario, the smaller hospitals struggle to allocate marketing budgets to bring about awareness amongst patients about their service.  On the other hand, the government has set itself a clear vision that while it wants to provide healthcare for its 1.3 bn people, it will only act as a “payor” and not a “provider”. It is obvious that when a government takes this position of a payor in a social industry such as healthcare, it is the recipe for price controls to come about. We are already seeing some of this playing out in the form of state and central schemes which define and limit pricing across multiple treatments.  Such controlled pricing can if at all manageable, can only be managed in smaller hospitals which are struggling to bring about awareness about their services. So we live in a dichotomy where low healthcare prices as defined by government regulation can be managed only in smaller hospitals but these small hospitals are struggling for survival. The ideal solution to this is consolidation. This is a similar scenario when OYO came in to consolidate the small hotels segment. MEDAGG is envisioned as one of the several models of aggregation that have started playing out as OYO equivalents in the healthcare space.” <h3>A FEW WORDS ABOUT VOH</h3> We wish Ramesh and Sumitha the very best in their efforts of bringing method in the madness of the customer’s decision making journey. As we proceed to conclude, we request them for their quick views on the Voice of Healthcare platform. The dynamic duo shares generously…  “VOH has taken up a commendable effort in bringing out to the knowledge of everyone, the innumerable innovations that are happening in the healthcare space. This is not only an encouragement for entrepreneurs but also a way to reach their products out to more and more audience!”|21954|2023-07-26 15:29:45|2023-07-26 09:59:45|closed|closed|transforming-medical-aggregation|publish|0|0|blog_post||0| | | |_wds_readability|a:4:{s:5:"score";i:56;s:9:"raw_score";i:56;s:11:"is_readable";b:0;s:5:"error";b:0;}| |

| | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |Reasons why you should use the Medagg Hospital Discovery Platform| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |&nbsp;  <img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-33551" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Downloader.la-65a10b797dd59-1024x384.jpg" alt="Piles Treatment Doctors In Chennai," width="800" height="300" />  &nbsp;  <strong>Elective Treatments / Surgeriesare best done after adequate research on hospital options from all angles</strong>  &nbsp;  Almost 70% of illnesses that need hospitalization are “elective” in nature; meaning, you can choose to have the treatment at your time of convenience (over a few weeks or months). In other words these treatments are not an emergency. For all such treatments, it is a wise practice to explore options available for you. This exploration will help you not only to get information about the right medical doctor but also all the information about hospitals so as to be empowered to choose the “ideal” option amongst numerous “good” options  &nbsp;  The purpose of the medagg platform is to help the patient with this awareness of multiple healthcare provider options at a single place along with the personalized guidance of an experienced healthcare management expert in the “care custodian”  &nbsp;  <strong>Comprehensive analysis of options is an arduous process if not done on a platform such as Medagg</strong>  &nbsp;  The process of exploring a specialist hospital is not an easy one without a common platform that brings all the hospitals together for comparison. The patient or patient family are either having to visit multiple hospitals personally to get details on treatment modality, cost, insurance, other hospital services, etc or having to visit multiple websites and make numerous phone calls. The search typically starts with something like “top hospitals in Chennai” on google or “treatment options for knee replacement surgery” or “average cost of total knee replacement”. Medagg brings the facility of a personal “care custodian” who can do this comparison for you and guide you through the exploration process step by step  &nbsp;  <strong>Tamil Nadu is great healthcare destination where you will find numerous options which are all “good” – but how do you know what is “ideal” for you?</strong>  &nbsp;  For many decades, Tamil Nadu has remained a Mecca for healthcare. But this could cause a “problem of plenty” – we have many “good” hospitals but how to I choose the “ideal” hospital that suits me? What are the factors that I should consider? The Medagg Care Custodian helps you navigate this process. Many aggregation platforms that are available today help find doctors or with appointment with the doctor. But the exploration of options for the patient does not stop only with the doctor’s advise. So the “search doctors” option that multiple aggregation platforms provide has been expanded to hospitals and their services by the Medagg platform. For example, when vicinity is an important consideration for patient convenience, why stop with a search like “physicians near me”. Medagg helps you with “hospitals near me”. In fact the Medagg mobile App tells you about hospitals near you automatically depending on your location.  &nbsp;  <strong>In the case of complex illnesses, you will also have to analyze treatment options apart from hospital options</strong>  &nbsp;  Sometimes treatment modalities could differ from clinician to clinician and hospital to hospital. One should ensure that he has gone through the pros and cons of all the modalities before choosing the right option. The common patient is not in a position to know these modalities and any amount of googling only confuses the patient more. This again is an area where the Madagg care custodians, who are experienced hospital operators, come in to help the patient make the wise decision.  &nbsp;  In this modern world of medicine, inter disciplinary treatment has come in to help patients in a big way. For example, there could be procedures that an interventional radiologist can do for a patient who is suffering from knee pain. Conventional wisdom will take the patient to the orthopedic doctor. But Medagg aims to bring about the awareness of new age treatments for the patient to feel empowerd to choose from.  &nbsp;  In certain cases, a patient may be advised for surgery but due to multiple reasons the patient may not be willing to go in for a surgery. However, there are other ways by which the patient’s pain may be alleviated even without having to go through surgery. Pain management as a field of medicine has advanced to great heights in this space.  &nbsp;  <strong>Cost is a key parameter to take into comparison apart from insurance acceptability, co-payment etc</strong>  &nbsp;  Cost optimization of treatment is an important factor to be considered in choosing the hospital. The common man does not know the nuances of cost optimization when it comes to medical treatment. The medagg care custodians who are experienced in the field of hospital management and financial counselling within hospitals help you optimize the cost of treatment for you. On an average, patients who have obtained treatment through the Medagg platform have ended up spending 30% less than what they would have otherwise spent. This is accomplished by multiple levers including the below: <ul>  	<li>Identifying a doctor of choice to do the surgery in a different hospital that he visits. The common patient may not be aware of this</li>  	<li>Identifying alternate providers for diagnostics as well as post-surgical recuperation / physiotherapy</li>  	<li>Identifying hospitals where the insured patient’s co-pay amount may be lower</li>  	<li>Identifying specific camps where a procedure is done within the patients budget</li> </ul> &nbsp;  <strong>Your second opinionshould be unbiased and you should feel empowered to take an informed choice on your treatment and hospital options</strong>  &nbsp;  We need to first of all understand (a) what is a second opinion (b) Why get a second opinion (c) How to get a second opinion and (d) can I get a second opinion from another doctor  &nbsp;  A second opinion meaning, “alternate medical opinion” is the right of any patient and it is legally covered under the patient rights and responsibilities in Indian law. Before a patient goes in for any complex treatment, it is always a good practice to get a second opinion. It is important to obtain such second opinions from hospitals and clinics which are not affiliated with the primary consultant doctor from where we got our first opinion. This is not because we cannot trust our doctors but to ensure that we have ensured that we have indeed explored everything needs to be understood about the treatment. Often times, there could be instances when a small change in the treatment modality from doctor to doctor might mean a lot to us and might make us shift towards a particular doctor  &nbsp;  In a lot of cases such second opinions can be obtained using just our medical report from the first opinion. Medagg can help find doctors from this category of who will be in a position to give such unbiased opinion. Online doctor consultations can also be organized to get a second opinion. This helps the patient avoid having to visit multiple hospitals to get such opinions. Many patients also choose to go through their general physician who can be a guide for them in finding the right second opinion doctor.  &nbsp;  Some of the common areas where we find patients look for second opinion include Cancer second opinion and Knee replacement second opinion. Medical second opinions and radiology second opinions are also quite common across multiple specialties.  &nbsp;  In summary, the Medagg platform can make the hospitalization journey a lot more smoother for patients while also helping the patient reduce the treatment cost substantially. Call Medagg at ……. Or write to us at …….. | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |Female Infertility due to Fallopian Tube Blockage – A rising concern| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="size-full wp-image-35588 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/1.png" alt="" width="624" height="416" />  Infertility is defined as being unable to get pregnant after a year of unprotected sex when the woman is within her reproductive age. There are various reasons why a woman experiences infertility.  Apart from abnormal ovulation, sperm count and motility, one of the common reasons for infertility is the blockage in fallopian tube(s).  Lately, studies and reports suggest that an increased number of people are undergoing infertility treatments and are battling with  high levels of family and societal stress.  <strong>Statistics by sex :</strong> <ul>  	<li>One-third of couples with infertility have an issue with the male partner</li>  	<li>One-third of the couples with infertility have an issue with the female partner</li>  	<li>One-third of the couples with infertility have an issue with both partners.</li> </ul> <strong>Why is infertility on the rise?</strong> <ul>  	<li>One of the main reasons why women experience infertility is the choice of a higher age to get pregnant. With an increase in age, the quality of eggs produced decreases</li>  	<li>The natural aging process also increases the chances of miscarriage.</li>  	<li>The quality of sperm decreases with men aged over 40.</li> </ul> <strong>Lifestyle Factors that play an important role in fertility :</strong> <ul>  	<li>Smoking tobacco can damage sperm quality and affect the reproductive hormones of both men and women.</li>  	<li>Alcohol too has an alarming effect on the reproductive system and is strictly prohibited during pregnancy.</li>  	<li>High levels of stress also leads to irregular menstrual cycles.</li> </ul> <strong>How Fallopian Tube Recanalization can help with infertility due to blocked fallopian tube(s)?</strong><img class="size-full wp-image-35589 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/2.png" alt="" width="454" height="303" />  Fallopian tube Recanalization is a procedure that does not involve an open surgery or laproscopic surgery. Instead an interventional radiologist uses a thin wire called a catheter through the cervix and the uterus to open the blockage.  <strong>The procedure involves:</strong> <ul>  	<li>Placing a speculum into the vagina and passing a small tube also known as a catheter through the cervix into the uterus.</li>  	<li>Examining the uterine cavity using an Xray camera.</li>  	<li>Determining the area of blockage in the tube</li>  	<li>Finally clearing the blockage using the catheter.</li> </ul> Over 90 % of the time the fallopian tube blockages can be removed which helps in increasing the chance of getting pregnant naturally and avoiding other fertility treatments such as IUI or IVF.  Also the success rate of FTR is high and studies have shown that 6 out of 10 women who have had issues with fertility have conceived naturally  <strong>Conclusion :</strong>  FTR is an innovative and highly successful procedure that has minimal side effects on the body.It has a high success rate and has helped a lot of women start off with motherhood naturally without any other interventions such as surgery, IUI and IVF  &nbsp;|35587|2024-05-29 11:29:05|2024-05-29 05:59:05|closed|closed|female-infertility-due-to-fallopian-tube-blockage-a-rising-concern|publish|0|0|blog_post||0| | | |_wds_readability|a:4:{s:5:"score";i:0;s:9:"raw_score";b:0;s:11:"is_readable";b:0;s:5:"error";s:19:"No content to check";}| |

| | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |Varicocele and why you should know about it?| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="size-full wp-image-35591 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/3.png" alt="" width="352" height="320" />  &nbsp;  <strong>What is it?</strong> <p style="text-align: justify;">Having a condition that results in a collection of enlarged veins in the scrotum (the bag that holds a man’s testicles) is known as Varicocele. Varicocele affects the veins that travel up towards the spermatic cord. The spermatic cord contains the tube that carries sperm from the testes to the penis, lymphatic vessels, and nerves. A varicocele might affect the development of the testicles and may result in decreased sperm count leading to infertility.</p> <strong>Symptoms of Varicocele </strong>  <img class="size-full wp-image-35592 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/4.png" alt="" width="624" height="410" />  Akshay – crop the top part of the pic saying “varicocele symptoms complications and treatment”  A varicocele often occurs on the left side of the scrotum and predominantly does not produce any signs or symptoms. However, possible indications might include :  Pain:     A stiff feeling down below which gets relieved when lying down.  Size:     A difference in the size of testicles might also be the result of this condition. Often the affected testicle may be smaller than the other one.  Infertility:   A varicocele might affect sperm count and reduce fertility but at the same time cannot be the only cause.  <img class="size-full wp-image-35593 aligncenter" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/5.png" alt="" width="381" height="299" />  <strong>Causes of Varicocele?</strong> <p style="text-align: justify;">There is no specific reason that causes this condition and doctors aren’t sure as to why it occurs. However, it usually takes place in teens because of their quick growth during puberty.  During development, the testicles need more blood than normal as they grow significantly in this stage and thereby any blockage might cause this condition.</p> <strong>Treatment :</strong>  Open Surgery : A typical surgery can help treat varicoceles. This is done under general anesthesia and will need several days/weeks for recovery.  Varicocele Embolization: Varicocele Embolization is a procedure that involves redirecting blood away from an enlarged vein in the scrotum. A radiologist uses a coil or special agents to block or embolize the vein. This can then improve the overall symptoms  What happens during the procedure?  The procedure usually takes a few hours and in general, you might expect the following : <ul>  	<li>You’ll be given medicine to make you feel comfortable, relaxed and sleepy first.</li>  	<li>Then you’ll receive a shot of numbing medicine into an area on the inner part of your upper thigh, this will prevent you from feeling much during the procedure.</li>  	<li>The health care provider will then clean the area, they will then put a needle into your inner thigh to access a major vein and they’ll insert the catheter tube into this vein.</li>  	<li>With the help of x-rays your provider will move the tube to the correct area in your scrotum and then a small coil or a special liquid will be inserted into the affected vein. This is called a blocking agent . This redirects the blood flow into other nearby veins and helps the blood to exit the scrotum normally</li>  	<li>After the procedure the catheter will be removed and a bandage will be placed on the area of entry on your thigh.</li> </ul> As far as recovery is concerned it is a lot quicker than a typical surgery given a couple of days of rest.  <strong>Take away :</strong>  If you have symptoms of varicocele talk to your doctor and find out what treatment suits you best at the same time don’t panic since this is completely treatable provided the right method is used.|35590|2024-05-29 11:37:53|2024-05-29 06:07:53|closed|closed|varicocele-and-why-you-should-know-about-it|publish|0|0|blog_post||0| | | |_wds_readability|a:4:{s:5:"score";i:0;s:9:"raw_score";b:0;s:11:"is_readable";b:0;s:5:"error";s:19:"No content to check";}| |

| | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |Signs of Pregnancy After Abortion "| Medagg Healthcare| | |Medagg| |Medagg| |<img class="alignnone wp-image-35687" src="https://medagghealthcare.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/Pregnancy-after-Abortion-1024x576.png" alt="Pregnancy after abortion" width="1273" height="716" />  <strong>Abortion</strong> is a medical procedure that terminates a pregnancy. One common method is medical abortion, which involves the use of medications to end a pregnancy. While it is a safe and effective method, it is important to understand the signs of pregnancy after abortion and the body’s response to the procedure. <h2>Signs of Pregnancy After Abortion</h2> After an abortion, it is possible to experience symptoms similar to those of a regular pregnancy, but it is important to differentiate between post-abortion symptoms and actual pregnancy symptoms. These symptoms can include: <ul>  	<li><strong>Swollen or Tender Breasts</strong>: Early stages of pregnancy can result in a wide range of hormonal fluctuations in the body. Swollen or tender breasts can also be an indication of the same.</li>  	<li>Due to the increase in blood flow and retention of fluids in the body, it is not uncommon for women to experience this symptom.</li>  	<li><strong>Bloating</strong>: It is a common symptom of early pregnancy and is a result of the hormonal changes that take place in the body. Water retention and slow digestive process can also be contributing factors to this symptom.</li>  	<li><strong>Nausea and Vomiting</strong>: Also known as morning sickness, nausea and vomiting is a normal part of pregnancy. It can occur during any time of the day, but most women feel a sense of queasiness as soon as they wake up.</li>  	<li><strong>Fatigue</strong>: Feeling tired can be another symptom during pregnancy as the body takes time to adapt to the changes that happen within. Fatigue can also be caused by other factors such as hormonal changes, increased blood flow, and low iron levels.</li>  	<li><strong>Constipation</strong>: Hormonal changes can be the key cause of multiple symptoms as mentioned and constipation can be a byproduct of the same. Medication, supplements, lack of fiber, and iron content in the diet can play a supporting role in contributing to this symptom as well.</li>  	<li><strong>Peeing More Often</strong>: When a woman conceives, the natural flow of blood increases and this increase in the blood flow to organs such as the kidneys provokes them to work harder thereby pushing out unwanted liquids in the form of urine more often.</li> </ul> <h2><strong>Pregnancy After having an Abortion ?</strong></h2> It is completely possible to get pregnant again soon after an abortion. Ovulation can occur as early as <strong>2</strong> weeks after the procedure, making it crucial to use contraception if you don’t want to get pregnant again immediately.  The timing of ovulation can vary depending on the individual’s menstrual cycle and the <h2>Safety of Getting Pregnant After an Abortion</h2> You can get pregnant again after having an abortion. However, it is crucial to give your body and mind time to recover completely before planning the next pregnancy.  If you experience any difficulties during or after the abortion, consult your healthcare provider before conceiving again. <h3>Body's Response After Abortion</h3> The body’s response after your abortion can vary depending on the type <ol>  	<li><strong>Bleeding and Cramping </strong>is quite common post abortion and lasts on an average of about a week or so depending on the individual and the chosen type of abortion.</li>  	<li><strong>Pain Relief - </strong>Your healthcare provider will equip you with certain medications to tackle the pain for a limited period of time.</li>  	<li><strong>Pelvic Rest - </strong>Avoiding strenuous activities and using sanitary pads rather than tampons can help reduce the risk of infection.</li> </ol> <h2><strong>When Is It Safe to Get Pregnant After Abortion?</strong></h2> <img src="https://images.surferseo.art/d35bd5e5-735c-4772-8501-c06a32ee851f.jpeg" />  There is no exact answer to this question, as it depends on various factors such as the individual's mental and physical health, type of abortion and time taken for recovery.  Nevertheless, an abortion does not affect the chances of a woman conceiving again. Consulting your healthcare provider before preparing for the next pregnancy could be a wise option. <h2>Conclusion</h2> Abortion is a safe and legal medical procedure that can be performed using either medical or surgical methods. Proper aftercare is crucial to ensure a smooth recovery.  If you're considering an abortion, consult a qualified healthcare provider and follow their instructions to minimize the risk of complications and maximize comfort. <h2><strong>FAQ's:</strong></h2> <h3><strong>1. How long does it take for hormones to settle after an abortion?</strong></h3> After an abortion, it can take a few weeks to a couple of months for hormone levels to stabilize. The body undergoes significant hormonal shifts as it adjusts to the absence of pregnancy.  During this time, most women experience mood swings, physical changes, and variations in their menstrual cycle. However, these hormonal fluctuations are normal and typically resolve over time.  <strong>2. When to expect period after abortion?</strong>  Most women can expect their menstrual period to return within <strong>4</strong> to <strong>6</strong> weeks after an abortion. This timeline can vary based on individual factors, including hormonal levels and overall health. <h3><strong>3. How to feel after an abortion?</strong></h3> The emotional aftermath of an abortion can vary widely. It is common for women to experience a complex mix of feelings, including relief, sadness, guilt, or anxiety.  The emotional response can depend on various factors, including personal beliefs, the circumstances surrounding the pregnancy, and the level of support available.  Seeking support from friends, family, or professional counsellors can be incredibly helpful in processing these emotions and navigating the recovery journey. <h3><strong>4. How long after a miscarriage or abortion can you get pregnant?</strong></h3> After a miscarriage or abortion, the possibility of becoming pregnant again can arise relatively quickly. It is possible to ovulate within a few weeks, which means that conception can happen almost immediately after the body resumes its normal menstrual cycle. <h3><strong>5. How do you balance hormones after an abortion?</strong></h3> Balancing hormones after an abortion can involve several strategies. Maintaining a healthy diet rich in whole foods, staying hydrated, and engaging in regular physical activity can support overall well-being and hormonal balance.  Additionally, managing stress through practices like mindfulness or yoga can also be beneficial. Consulting with a healthcare provider can offer tailored advice to support recovery during this phase. <h3><strong>6. How do you know if your uterus is damaged?</strong></h3> Concerns about uterine health following an abortion are valid. Signs of potential complications include severe abdominal pain, excessive bleeding, or persistent fever.  If any of these symptoms occur, it’s essential to seek medical attention promptly.  Healthcare professionals can use ultrasounds or other assessments to evaluate uterine health and ensure there are no lingering issues. <h3><strong>7. What are the five elements of post-abortion care?</strong></h3> <strong>Post-abortion care</strong> is vital to ensure physical and emotional recovery. This care typically includes several key elements. <ul>  	<li><strong>First</strong>, a physical health assessment is crucial to monitor recovery and identify any potential complications.</li>  	<li><strong>Second</strong>, providing emotional support is essential, as many women experience a range of feelings after an abortion.</li>  	<li><strong>Third</strong>, discussing contraceptive options helps prevent unintended pregnancies in the future.</li>  	<li><strong>Fourth</strong>, follow-up care is important to check on the woman’s physical and emotional well-being.</li>  	<li><strong>Lastly</strong>, educating women about future pregnancies is critical, helping them understand their reproductive health and what to expect moving forward.</li> </ul> <strong>8. Can I do exercise after an abortion?</strong>  Regarding physical activity, many women wonder if they can resume exercise after an abortion. Generally, light exercise can be resumed within a few days after the procedure, but it’s essential to listen to one’s body and avoid strenuous activities until fully healed.  Consulting a healthcare provider for personalized recommendations can provide clarity on when it’s completely safe to return to regular exercise routines. <h3><strong>9. Will I be able to conceive after an abortion?</strong></h3> Yes, most women can conceive after an abortion without issues. Having an abortion does not create barriers to future conception, and studies indicate that the risk of complications in future pregnancies remains low.  However, maintaining regular health check-ups is crucial to ensure overall reproductive health. <h3><strong>10. How many days after abortion periods come?</strong></h3> Typically, women can expect their period to return within <strong>4</strong> to <strong>6</strong> weeks after an abortion. This timing can vary based on individual circumstances and hormonal fluctuations. <h3><strong>11. What causes delay in period after abortion?</strong></h3> Delays in the menstrual cycle can be attributed to various factors, including hormonal imbalances or the presence of retained pregnancy tissue.  It is crucial to communicate with a healthcare provider if periods are significantly delayed to rule out any potential complications. <h3><strong>12. Is it normal to have a lighter period after an abortion?</strong></h3> Yes, lighter periods can occur after an abortion due to hormonal changes and the body’s adapting process. It is a common experience, but if there are any concerns about menstrual changes, consulting a healthcare provider is advisable. <h3><strong>13. What should you do if you have undergone an abortion?</strong></h3> If you have undergone an abortion, it is important to follow specific recommendations to ensure a smooth recovery. Rest and avoid strenuous activities for a few days. Monitor for any signs of complications such as severe pain, excessive bleeding, or fever, and seek medical attention if these occur. Start contraception as advised by your healthcare provider to prevent unintended pregnancies. Wait to have sex until you feel physically and emotionally ready, and consider seeking post-abortion care to address any emotional or physical concerns.|35685|2024-07-25 17:55:37|2024-07-25 12:25:37|closed|closed|signs-of-pregnancy-after-abortion|publish|0|0|blog_post||0| | | |_wds_readability|a:4:{s:5:"score";i:52;s:9:"raw_score";i:52;s:11:"is_readable";b:0;s:5:"error";b:0;}| |
